<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries by freshwater withdrawal</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>

<p>This is a <b>list of countries by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Freshwater_withdrawal" title="Freshwater withdrawal">freshwater withdrawal</a></b> mostly based on <a href="/wiki/The_World_Factbook" title="The World Factbook">The World Factbook</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> accessed in June 2008. 
</p>
